[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA stack-buffer-overflow vulnerability has been detected in the Wireshark codebase [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mduring fuzzing of the BER [0m[1;39m([0m[39mBasic Encoding Rules[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m dissector. The issue occurs in the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`dissect_ber_GeneralString` function where a [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte write operation overflows a [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstack-allocated buffer named `name_string`. This is a memory safety vulnerability [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith a SCARINESS score of [0m[1;36m46[0m[39m, classified as a [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte-write-stack-buffer-overflow.[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Vulnerability Type[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis is an **AddressSanitizer: stack-buffer-overflow** vulnerability, specifically [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39ma [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte write operation that underflows a stack-allocated buffer.[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Issue Details[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability manifests during the execution of the BER handler fuzzer with the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfollowing characteristics:[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Location of the Overflow**: The overflow occurs at address `[0m[1;36m0x7ffe384e945f[0m[39m` [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mduring a WRITE operation of size [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m in the `dissect_ber_GeneralString` function at [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mline [0m[1;36m3194[0m[39m, column [0m[1;36m34[0m[39m of `[0m[35m/src/wireshark/epan/dissectors/[0m[95mpacket-ber.c[0m[39m`.[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Stack Frame Analysis**: The problematic memory access occurs in the [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`try_dissect_unknown_ber` function's stack frame, which contains [0m[1;36m12[0m[39m stack-allocated[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mobjects. The access at offset [0m[1;36m159[0m[39m underflows the `name_string` variable, which is [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocated at offsets [0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m160[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m240[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - an [0m[1;36m80[0m[39m-byte buffer starting at offset [0m[1;36m160[0m[39m in the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstack frame.[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Call Stack**: The vulnerability is triggered through the following execution [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpath:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `dissect_ber_GeneralString` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhere the actual overflow write occurs[0m[1;39m)[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `try_dissect_unknown_ber` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhere the vulnerable buffer is allocated[0m[1;39m)[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `call_dissector_through_handle` and `call_dissector_work` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdissector [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mframework[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `call_all_postdissectors` and `dissect_frame` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpacket processing[0m[1;39m)[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `epan_dissect_run` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mEPAN dissection engine[0m[1;39m)[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfuzzer entry point[0m[1;39m)[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Memory Access Pattern**: The shadow bytes analysis reveals that the memory at [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moffset [0m[1;36m159[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmarked as `f2` - Stack mid redzone[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is accessed, which is one byte [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbefore the start of the `name_string` buffer at offset [0m[1;36m160[0m[39m. This indicates an [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moff-by-one error or incorrect bounds checking when writing to the buffer.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Important Observations[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Buffer Underflow**: The issue is specifically a buffer underflow [0m[1;39m([0m[39maccessing [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmemory before the buffer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m rather than an overflow [0m[1;39m([0m[39maccessing memory after the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, as the access at offset [0m[1;36m159[0m[39m is one byte before the buffer starting at [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moffset [0m[1;36m160[0m[39m.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Stack Variables in Context**: The `try_dissect_unknown_ber` function allocates[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmultiple local variables including:[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `name_string` [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m80[0m[39m bytes at offset [0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m160[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m240[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `asn1_ctx` [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m208[0m[39m bytes at offset [0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m272[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m480[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Several exception handling structures[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Various BER-related metadata fields [0m[1;39m([0m[39mclass, pc, tag, len[0m[1;39m)[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Reproducer Input**: The fuzzer identified a specific input pattern that [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtriggers this vulnerability, shown in both hexadecimal and escaped string formats [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min the output.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3084[0m[39m:            [0m[1;35mdissect_unknown_ber[0m[1;39m([0m[39mactx->pinfo, tvb, hoffset, unknown_tree[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3085[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3086[0m[39m:        return end_offset;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3087[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3088[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3089[0m[39m:    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlen >= [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmax_len - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3090[0m[39m:        len = max_len - [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3091[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3092[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3093[0m[39m:    [0m[1;35mtvb_memcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, str, offset, len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3094[0m[39m:    str[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mlen[0m[1;39m][0m[39m=[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3095[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3096[0m[39m:    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mhf_id > [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3097[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35mproto_tree_add_string[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtree, hf_id, tvb, offset, len, str[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3098[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3099[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3100[0m[39m:    return end_offset;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3101[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis Summary[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability is a stack-buffer-underflow in the `dissect_ber_GeneralString` [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunction at line [0m[1;36m3194[0m[39m of `epan/dissectors/packet-ber.c`. The root cause involves [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtwo critical bugs:[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Incorrect buffer and offset usage [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m3188[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**: The code reads a length value[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfrom the wrong buffer at the wrong offset:[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```c[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   tvb_len = [0m[1;35mtvb_get_uint8[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, offset[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   After `dissect_ber_restricted_string` returns at line [0m[1;36m3179[0m[39m:[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `offset` has advanced past the entire BER structure in the original `tvb`[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `out_tvb` is a NEW buffer containing ONLY the decoded string data[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Reading from `tvb` at the advanced `offset` returns arbitrary/garbage data[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Incorrect type declaration [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m3177[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**: The `tvb_len` variable is declared [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mas `int8_t`, which means byte values [0m[1;36m0x80[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m0xFF[0m[39m become negative [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m-128[0m[39m to [0m[1;36m-1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m when [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstored.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Buffer underflow [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m3194[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**: When `tvb_len` is negative [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m[1;36m-1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcode writes to `name_string[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mtvb_len[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`, which accesses memory before the buffer [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstart:[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```c[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   name_string[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mtvb_len[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m When tvb_len = [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m, writes to name_string[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m-1[0m[1;39m][0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe AddressSanitizer report confirms this: the write at offset [0m[1;36m159[0m[39m is one byte [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbefore the `name_string` buffer starting at offset [0m[1;36m160[0m[39m.[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Primary Changes to `dissect_ber_GeneralString` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m3172[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3199[0m[1;39m)[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Change the type of `tvb_len` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m3177[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Replace `int8_t tvb_len;` with `unsigned tvb_len;`[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This matches the return type of `[0m[1;35mtvb_reported_length[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and prevents negative [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalues[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Consistent with the `unsigned name_len` parameter[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Fix the length retrieval [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m3188[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Replace `tvb_len = [0m[1;35mtvb_get_uint8[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, offset[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;` with `tvb_len = [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mtvb_reported_length[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This reads the actual length from the correct buffer [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`out_tvb`[0m[1;39m)[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Follows the pattern used throughout the codebase [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`dissect_ber_octet_string_wcb` at line [0m[1;36m1803[0m[39m, `packet-dap.[0m[1;92mc:1543[0m[39m`, [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`packet-x509if.[0m[1;92mc:738[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Remove unnecessary cast [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m3189[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Change `if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39munsigned[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mtvb_len >= name_len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb_len >= name_len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The cast is no longer needed since `tvb_len` is now `unsigned`[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m: Fix null termination when truncating [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m3190[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3191[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- When the decoded string is too large for the buffer, ensure null termination at [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe correct position:[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- After copying `name_len-[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m` bytes, add: `name_string[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mname_len-[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;`[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This ensures the buffer is always properly null-terminated within bounds[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Complete Corrected Code Block[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mReplace lines [0m[1;36m3176[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3195[0m[39m with:[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtvbuff_t *out_tvb = NULL;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munsigned tvb_len;[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moffset = [0m[1;35mdissect_ber_restricted_string[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfalse, BER_UNI_TAG_GeneralString, actx, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtree, tvb, offset, hf_id, [0m[1;39m([0m[39mname_string[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ? &out_tvb : NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mname_string[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        tvb_len = [0m[1;35mtvb_reported_length[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb_len >= name_len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;35mtvb_memcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb, [0m[1;39m([0m[39muint8_t*[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mname_string, [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, name_len-[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            name_string[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mname_len-[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;35mtvb_memcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb, [0m[1;39m([0m[39muint8_t*[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mname_string, [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, tvb_len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            name_string[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mtvb_len[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This Is Optimal[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Follows established patterns**: The fix uses `[0m[1;35mtvb_reported_length[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhich is the standard pattern throughout the Wireshark codebase for getting the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlength of decoded data from a tvbuff.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Preserves existing functionality**: The fix maintains the same logic flow:[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Delegates BER parsing to `dissect_ber_restricted_string`[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Optionally copies decoded data to caller-provided buffer[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Performs bounds checking and truncation if needed[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Always null-terminates the output string[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Matches the old implementation's correctness**: The disabled old [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimplementation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m3040[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3101[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m shows the correct pattern of bounds checking [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbefore null termination. The fix applies this same logic to the new implementation.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Minimal invasive changes**: Only modifies the buggy section [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m3177[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3194[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mleaving the rest of the function and all callers unchanged.[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Preserves Existing Logic[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Maintains API compatibility**: The function signature remains unchanged, so [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mall [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m call site at line [0m[1;36m935[0m[39m continues to work without modification.[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Supports same use cases**: [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - When `name_string` is NULL: no copying occurs [0m[1;39m([0m[39mjust dissection[0m[1;39m)[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - When `name_string` is provided: copies decoded data with truncation if needed[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Preserves BER parsing**: The call to `dissect_ber_restricted_string` at line [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3179[0m[39m remains unchanged, maintaining all BER protocol handling.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Addresses the Issue[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Eliminates buffer underflow**: By using the actual decoded length from [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`out_tvb`, the value is always non-negative and represents real data length, [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpreventing negative indexing.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Fixes incorrect buffer access**: Reads from the correct buffer [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`out_tvb`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minstead of the wrong buffer [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`tvb`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m at the wrong offset.[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Ensures proper bounds checking**: The comparison `tvb_len >= name_len` now [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muses the actual decoded string length, ensuring truncation logic works correctly.[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Guarantees null termination within bounds**: Both code paths [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtruncated and [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnon-truncated[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m correctly null-terminate within the buffer bounds.[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Potential Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Change in behavior when decoded string length exceeds buffer size**: [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Old buggy code: would use arbitrary garbage as length, potentially causing [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munderflow or other memory corruption[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - New fixed code: properly truncates to `name_len-[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m` bytes and null-terminates [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mat `name_len-[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m`[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Impact**: This is the correct behavior that matches the old disabled [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimplementation and prevents memory corruption[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Type change from `int8_t` to `unsigned`**:[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All comparisons and indexing operations now use unsigned arithmetic[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Since lengths are inherently non-negative, this is semantically correct[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Impact**: No negative side effects; improves type safety[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **No impact on callers**: The function signature is unchanged, and the single [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcaller at line [0m[1;36m935[0m[39m passes `[0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname_string[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` = [0m[1;36m80[0m[39m, which works correctly with [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe fix.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Similar Solutions in Codebase[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix follows the exact pattern used in multiple places:[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **`dissect_ber_octet_string_wcb` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m1803[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**:[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```c[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfunc && out_tvb && [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtvb_reported_length[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m > [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **`packet-dap.c` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m1543[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**:[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```c[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   len = [0m[1;35mtvb_reported_length[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **`packet-x509if.c` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m738[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**:[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```c[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   value = [0m[1;35mtvb_format_text[0m[1;39m([0m[39mactx->pinfo->pool, out_tvb, [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mtvb_reported_length[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAll these examples consistently use `[0m[1;35mtvb_reported_length[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to get the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdecoded data length after calling a BER dissection function that returns an [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`out_tvb`.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
